Finally, the location of the hotel is a few steps away from the Shanxi Merchants Museum (free advance reservation). msg:A typical old five-star hotel. Although the hardware is relatively old, it is clean and hygienic. Even though it is old, the materials used at that time were also very particular, and there was no cracking of the wood or deformation of the cabinet door.
The software is simply amazing. The balloons that the children bought in the ancient town accidentally flew to the roof nearly 10 meters high. The hotel staff took a long time to dispatch the electric lift. They had many reasons to refuse the ten-yuan balloons and refused to give them. They were looking for trouble, but they saw the longing eyes of the children. In addition, call in advance and prepare children's toothbrushes, slippers and disposable bathtub bags. It shows thoughtfulness in every aspect and spends a small amount of money to do big things. Details determine success or failure. I fell in love with the city of Taiyuan unconsciously.
The location of the hotel is also very good. Turn left 200 meters away from the Shanxi Merchants Museum. Opposite the museum is the Bell and Drum Tower Snack Street. Next door is Fuxi Street Subway Station. It takes 15 minutes to take a taxi to the Provincial Museum. Lao Taiyuan Restaurant is on the right when you go out. For this location and service, this is the right place to choose when you come to Taiyuan.

msg:The location is quite good, very close to Liuxiang, where there is a large night market, and I go there for a walk every night. I booked this hotel because I saw it was very high and could overlook Taiyuan. Unfortunately, the sky was always gray and the air in the city was not very good.

This hotel is above many financial institutions. The 1st to 4th floors are financial institutions, and the 6th to 30th floors are office buildings. Fortunately, the elevators run separately in the high and low areas, so you won't have to face the dilemma of squeezing into the elevator with office workers. However, this hotel is still a bit too business-like for us. Most of the guests are middle-aged men. Going back to the hotel every day feels like a business trip, M said.

By the way, the hotel is not very new, so it looks a bit old. For example, there are some old stains on the toilet floor that cannot be removed. I started to feel uncomfortable with Xiaodu's company in the guest room. After staying there for three days, I started to feel quite nostalgic.
